			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales by segment as a percent of total net sales for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fourth</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter were as follows: for the Americas</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">47</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">; for EMEA, 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and for Asia-Pacific, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">14</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in the Americas </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">decreased</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> 5 percent in the fourth quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to lower sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Multi-Use Product</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the United States and Canada which decreased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">17</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent, respectively.&nbsp;&nbsp;In the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, we experienced strong demand for </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Multi-Use Product </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in the United States and Canada </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">linked to renovation trends associated with the pandemic.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Although demand for our maintenance products in the United States remained strong in the fourth quarter of this fiscal year, we were unable to meet this demand due</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> to continued supply chain constraints and disruptions related to the COVID-19 pandemic.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;"> These declines were partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;">higher sales of maintenance products in Latin America.&nbsp; 			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>

			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in EMEA increased 6 percent in the fourth quarter. Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had a favorable impact on sales for the EMEA segment from period to period. On a constant currency basis, sales for the fourth quarter would have decreased by 6 percent compared to the prior fiscal year quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;This </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">constant currency </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales decline was driven by lower sales in the EMEA direct markets</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">which</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> were partially offset by increased sales in our EMEA distributor markets. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;">T</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">he </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increase in sales in the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> EMEA distributor markets were primarily driven by the easing of COVID-19 lockdown measures and restrictions.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The decrease in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> sales in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the EMEA direct markets was due to much higher sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> comparable</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the fourth quarter of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fiscal</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> 2020</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> due to the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> lifting of</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> severe COVID-19 lockdown measures tha</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">t</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> occurred during the third quarter of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">last </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">year </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">that</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> resulted in higher consumer demand in the fourth quarter of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">last year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;">Net sales in Asia-Pacific increased 32 percent in the fourth quarter primarily due to higher sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;">WD-40 Multi-Use Product</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;"> in the Asia distributor markets</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;"> which increased 1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;">98</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;"> percent </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">compared to the prior year fiscal </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;background-color: #FFFFFF;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;T</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">hese sales increases were primarily driven by the easing of COVID-19 lockdown measures and restrictions</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. Th</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ese reduced lockdown measures positively impacted economic conditions during the fourth quarter and resulted in increased demand and higher sales particularly in South Korea and Indonesia.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company owns a wide range of maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;,&nbsp;Lava&#xAE;</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and Solvol&#xAE;. &nbsp;</font>
